I was an ex employee of LTI. From 2020 batch. I was given java domain. Spring boot, JSP, angular, maven, oracle SQL training was given. At the end we were made to do a project. We were divided into teams and topic was given. This phase is called gladiators phase. After this i was alloted to Citi Bank project. I was happy and hopeful that i was allocated to Citi Bank. Till this this point I was in an impression that LTI is a good company. Now the disaster starts after this. I was waiting for work. We were batch of 60 and we were initially told to learn python. I was confused as we were told we would work on backend on Citibank and develop APIs. I started learning python and after some time they told to learn MS Excel. 4 months had passed by that time. We were also made to do OCAJP certification that is oracle certified java associate. After being 4 months without work i asked my manager he told we are working on it. I approached many managers, and assistant directors as well as HRs but none helped me. Finally I got work after 7 months. I was very disappointed with the work. My work was to send survey links and make people fill it and gather answers. Next day of getting this work i resigned. I used these 7 months to prepare and got in to good product based company with way high CTC than LTI. Management of LTI treated me as garbage after resignation. The took 2lakh bond from me though I had been at LTI for 1.3 yrs. Fortunately new organisation paid my bond. Join LTI to regret later.

#include <iostream>
#include<string>
using namespace std ;

main()
{
int count=0;
int a[26]={};  // making empty array of 26 elements 

 string s;
 getline(cin,s);
 int l=s.length();
 for (int i=0;i<l;i++){
     if(s[i]>=65 && s[i]<=90)
     {
         a[((int)s[i])-65]=1;
     }
     else if(s[i]>=97 && s[i]<=122)
     {
         a[((int)s[i])-97]=1;
     }
     
     
 }
 
 for(int i=0;i<26;i++)
 {
     if(s[i]==0)
     {
         count++;
     }
 }
 if(count==0)
 {
     cout<<"anagram";
 }
 else
 {
     cout<<"non";
 }
 
}

st=input("Enter the string:")
lst=[]
f=0
for i in range(26):
    lst.append(0)
for i in range(len(st)):
    if st[i]==" ":
        continue
    lst[ord(st[i].upper())-65]+=1
for i in lst:
    if i==0:
        f=1
        break
if f==1:
    print("{} is not panagram".format(st))
else:
    print("{} is panagram".format(st))

for i in range(n*n):
    a.append(int(input()))

c=[]
for i in a2:

        c.extend(i)

# Display the matrix in snake order

r=int(input("enter the number of row"))
c=int(input("enter number of column"))

matrix = []
for i in range(r):
    a=[]
    for j in range(0,c):
        a.append(int(input()))
    matrix.append(a)
# print matrix
for i in range(r):
    for j in range(c):
        print(matrix[i][j],end=" ")
    print()

print("In snake order")
#print in snake pattern
for i in range(r):
    if i == 0 or i %2== 0:
        for j in range(0,c):
            print(matrix[i][j], end= " ")

    if i % 2 !=0:
        for j in reversed(range(c)):
            print(matrix[i][j], end=" ")

    print()

import numpy as np
n=int(input())
l=[ ]
for i in range(n):
    for j in range(n):
        l.append(int(input()))
a=np.asarray(l)
a=np.reshape(a,(n,n))
for i in range(n):
    for j in range(n):
        if i%2==0:
            print(a[i][j],end=" ")
        else:
            print(a[i][-j-1],end=" ")

the code in python


for i in range(int(input())):
    a = int(input())
    b = list(map(int,input().split()))
    c=0
    d=0
    e=[]
    for i in range(len(b)):
        if(c%2==0 and d!=a):
            print(b[i],end=' ')
            d+=1
        elif(c%2==1 and d!=a):
            e.append(b[i])
            d+=1
        if(d==a and c%2==1):
            e=e[::-1]
            for j in e:
                print(j,end=' ')
            d=0
            c+=1
            e=[]
        elif(d==a):
            d=0
            c+=1
    print()
